    SELECT DISTINCT [t].*
    FROM (
        SELECT TOP(1) [proj.Context0].[Id]
        FROM [Projects] AS [proj0]
        INNER JOIN [Contexts] AS [proj.Context0] ON [proj0].[ContextId] = [proj.Context0].[Id]
        WHERE [proj0].[Id] = @__id_0

) AS [t0] ON [proj.Context.ScreenLinks].[ContextEntityId] = [t0].[Id]

    INNER JOIN [Contexts] AS [project.Context0] ON [project0].[ContextId] = [project.Context0].[Id]
) AS [t] ON [project.Context.ScreenLinks].[ContextEntityId] = [t].[Id]
ORDER BY [t].[Id]
